##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 1
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") defines "Confidential Information" as any non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party"), whether in written, oral, electronic, or other form, that is designated as confidential or that reasonably should be understood to be confidential given the nature of the information or the circumstances of disclosure. Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, trade secrets, business strategies, financial data, product designs, technical specifications, software code, marketing plans, customer lists, supplier information, and any other information that derives independent economic value from not being generally known to the public.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all copies, extracts, summaries, or analyses of such information, regardless of who prepares them. Confidential Information does not include information that: (a) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Receiving Party; (b) was lawfully known to the Receiving Party prior to disclosure by the Disclosing Party; (c) is rightfully obtained by the Receiving Party from a third party without breach of any confidentiality obligation; or (d) is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reliance on or reference to the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information.  

The Receiving Party acknowledges that the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information is valuable and unique, and its unauthorized use or disclosure could cause irreparable harm. Accordingly, the Receiving Party agrees to exercise the same degree of care to protect the Confidential Information as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but in no event less than reasonable care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: The Receiving Party may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a potential business relationship with the Disclosing Party, as explicitly agreed in writing.  

2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying composition or design.  

3. **No Unauthorized Copies**: The Receiving Party shall not make copies of Confidential Information except as strictly necessary for the Authorized Purpose, and all copies must bear the same confidentiality markings as the original.  

4. **Restricted Access**: Confidential Information shall only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or agents of the Receiving Party who have a need to know and who are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as those herein.  

5. **No Public Disclosure**: The Receiving Party shall not disclose Confidential Information to any third party without the Disclosing Party’s prior written consent.  

6. **No Competitive Use**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to develop, market, or sell products or services competitive with those of the Disclosing Party.  

7. **Secure Storage**: Confidential Information shall be stored in a secure location, protected by physical and electronic safeguards to prevent unauthorized access.  

8. **No Modification**: The Receiving Party shall not alter or modify Confidential Information without the Disclosing Party’s express written permission.  

9. **Notification of Breach**: The Receiving Party shall immediately notify the Disclosing Party upon discovering any unauthorized use or disclosure of Confidential Information.  

10. **Return or Destruction**: Upon the Disclosing Party’s request or termination of this Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  

11. **No Implied License**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Receiving Party any license, ownership, or rights to the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information beyond the Authorized Purpose.  

12. **Compliance with Laws**: The Receiving Party shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection and export control laws.  

13. **No Misrepresentation**: The Receiving Party shall not misrepresent the origin or ownership of Confidential Information or claim any rights to it.  

14. **No Solicitation**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to solicit the Disclosing Party’s employees, customers, or suppliers.  

15. **No Transfer**: The Receiving Party shall not assign, transfer, or sublicense its rights or obligations under this Agreement without the Disclosing Party’s prior written consent.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the Effective Date (the "Term"). Upon mutual written agreement, the parties may renew the Term for additional periods under terms to be negotiated in good faith. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing thirty (30) days’ prior written notice to the other party. Notwithstanding termination, the Receiving Party’s obligations with respect to Confidential Information shall survive for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] from the date of disclosure or such longer period as required by law. The Disclosing Party may also terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Receiving Party breaches any material provision of this Agreement and fails to cure such breach within fifteen (15) days of receiving notice. Upon termination, the Receiving Party shall cease all use of Confidential Information and, as directed by the Disclosing Party, return or destroy all copies. The obligations of confidentiality, non-use, and non-disclosure shall survive termination indefinitely for trade secrets and for the duration specified above for other Confidential Information.  

#part 4  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert jurisdiction, e.g., the State of New York], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert city, e.g., New York City], and the arbitral award shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts located in [insert venue, e.g., New York County, New York] for such purposes. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 2
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential information (the "Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, all non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information disclosed in written, oral, electronic, or any other form, whether marked as confidential or not, that is related to the Discloser’s business, operations, products, services, or intellectual property.  

The scope of Confidential Information encompasses: (a) trade secrets, technical data, research, development, and manufacturing processes; (b) business strategies, marketing plans, financial information, and customer or supplier lists; (c) software, algorithms, inventions, patents, and unpublished patent applications; (d) any other information that, by its nature or the circumstances of its disclosure, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

Confidential Information does not include information that: (i) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Recipient; (ii) was rightfully known to the Recipient prior to disclosure by the Discloser; (iii) is independently developed by the Recipient without reliance on the Discloser’s Confidential Information; or (iv) is lawfully obtained from a third party without restriction on disclosure.  

The Recipient agrees to treat all Confidential Information with the same degree of care as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than reasonable care. The Recipient shall not disclose, reproduce, or use Confidential Information for any purpose other than the permitted uses outlined in this Agreement.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: The Recipient may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship with the Discloser, as mutually agreed in writing.  

2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components or methodologies.  

3. **No Unauthorized Disclosure**: The Recipient shall not disclose Confidential Information to any third party without the Discloser’s prior written consent.  

4. **Internal Access**: Confidential Information may only be accessed by the Recipient’s employees, contractors, or agents who have a legitimate need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  

5. **No Copying**: The Recipient shall not copy, duplicate, or reproduce Confidential Information except as necessary for the authorized purpose and with the Discloser’s consent.  

6. **Security Measures**: The Recipient shall implement and maintain reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

7. **No Publicity**: The Recipient shall not use the Discloser’s name, trademarks, or Confidential Information in any press release, advertisement, or promotional material without prior written approval.  

8. **No Competitive Use**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to develop, market, or sell products or services competitive with the Discloser’s offerings.  

9. **Return or Destruction**: Upon the Discloser’s request or termination of this Agreement, the Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  

10. **No Implied License**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Recipient any license or right to use the Discloser’s intellectual property beyond the authorized purpose.  

11. **Compliance with Laws**: The Recipient shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection and export control laws.  

12. **No Misrepresentation**: The Recipient shall not misrepresent the origin or ownership of Confidential Information or claim any rights to it.  

13. **Notification of Breach**: The Recipient shall immediately notify the Discloser in writing upon discovering any unauthorized disclosure or breach of this Agreement.  

14. **No Transfer of Rights**: The Recipient shall not assign, transfer, or sublicense its rights or obligations under this Agreement without the Discloser’s prior written consent.  

15. **Survival of Obligations**: The Recipient’s confidentiality obligations shall survive termination of this Agreement for as long as the Confidential Information remains protected under applicable law.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the effective date (the "Term"), unless earlier terminated as provided herein. The Term may be renewed by mutual written agreement of the parties. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing written notice to the other party, with such termination becoming effective upon receipt of the notice. Upon termination, the Recipient’s obligations under this Agreement shall continue with respect to any Confidential Information disclosed prior to termination.  

The Discloser may terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Recipient breaches any of its obligations hereunder and fails to cure such breach within [insert cure period, e.g., thirty (30) days] of receiving written notice. Termination of this Agreement shall not relieve the Recipient of its obligations to protect Confidential Information disclosed during the Term. All provisions of this Agreement that, by their nature, should survive termination (including but not limited to confidentiality obligations, return or destruction of Confidential Information, and dispute resolution) shall survive.  

#part 4  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert governing law jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its then-current rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert arbitration venue, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the arbitrator’s award shall be final and binding. Judgment on the award may be entered in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts located in [insert court venue, e.g., the County of San Francisco, California] for such purposes.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 3
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information (collectively, "Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, all non-public, sensitive, or proprietary information, whether disclosed orally, in writing, electronically, or by any other means. This encompasses trade secrets, business strategies, financial data, technical specifications, product designs, software code, customer lists, marketing plans, and any other information marked as confidential or which, by its nature, should reasonably be understood as confidential.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all derivatives, analyses, compilations, or summaries created by the Recipient based on the disclosed information. It also includes any information shared during meetings, presentations, or discussions related to the business relationship between the parties. Confidential Information excludes information that: (a) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Recipient; (b) was lawfully in the Recipient’s possession prior to disclosure by the Discloser; (c) is independently developed by the Recipient without reliance on the Discloser’s Confidential Information; or (d) is rightfully obtained by the Recipient from a third party without breach of confidentiality obligations.  

The Recipient acknowledges the sensitive nature of the Confidential Information and agrees to exercise the same degree of care as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than a reasonable standard of care. Unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information may cause irreparable harm to the Discloser, entitling the Discloser to seek injunctive relief in addition to other legal remedies.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: The Recipient may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship with the Discloser, as mutually agreed in writing.  
2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components or methodologies.  
3. **No Unauthorized Copies**: The Recipient shall not make copies of Confidential Information except as necessary for the authorized purpose, and all copies must bear the same confidentiality markings as the original.  
4. **Restricted Access**: Confidential Information shall only be accessible to employees, contractors, or agents of the Recipient who have a legitimate need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as stringent as those herein.  
5. **No Public Disclosure**: The Recipient shall not disclose Confidential Information to the public, media, or any third party without the Discloser’s prior written consent.  
6. **No Competitive Use**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to gain a competitive advantage over the Discloser or to develop competing products or services.  
7. **Security Measures**: The Recipient shall implement appropriate physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or theft.  
8. **Notification of Breach**: The Recipient shall promptly notify the Discloser upon discovering any unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information.  
9. **Return or Destroy**: Upon the Discloser’s request or termination of the Agreement, the Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  
10. **No License Granted**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Recipient any license, ownership, or rights to the Discloser’s Confidential Information beyond the scope of this Agreement.  
11. **Compliance with Laws**: The Recipient shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection and privacy laws.  
12. **No Solicitation**: The Recipient shall not solicit the Discloser’s employees, customers, or partners using Confidential Information obtained under this Agreement.  
13. **No Modification**: The Recipient shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works based on Confidential Information without the Discloser’s express written permission.  
14. **Third-Party Disclosures**: The Recipient shall not disclose Confidential Information to any third party, including subcontractors, without the Discloser’s prior written approval.  
15. **Audit Rights**: The Discloser may audit the Recipient’s compliance with this Agreement upon reasonable notice and during normal business hours.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the Effective Date (the "Term"). The Term may be renewed by mutual written agreement of the parties. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing written notice to the other party, with such termination becoming effective immediately upon receipt of the notice. However, the obligations of confidentiality shall survive termination for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] or as required by applicable law, whichever is longer. Upon termination, the Recipient shall cease all use of Confidential Information and, as directed by the Discloser, return or destroy all copies of Confidential Information in its possession or control. The Discloser may request a written certification of destruction from the Recipient. Certain provisions, including those relating to ownership, audit rights, and dispute resolution, shall survive termination indefinitely. Termination of this Agreement shall not relieve the parties of any obligations arising prior to termination.  

#part 4  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association (AAA)] under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert city, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in connection with such dispute. The parties irrevocably waive any right to a jury trial and agree to arbitrate solely on an individual basis, not as part of a class or consolidated action.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 4
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information (collectively, "Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, all non-public, sensitive, or proprietary information, whether disclosed orally, in writing, electronically, or by any other means, that is marked or identified as confidential or that, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

Confidential Information encompasses, without limitation: (a) business strategies, financial data, pricing models, and marketing plans; (b) technical data, trade secrets, inventions, patents, and research; (c) software, algorithms, source code, and proprietary technology; (d) customer lists, supplier details, and contractual terms; (e) product designs, prototypes, and manufacturing processes; and (f) any other information that derives independent economic value from not being generally known to the public.  

The scope of this Agreement extends to all forms of Confidential Information, whether disclosed before or after the effective date of this Agreement, and includes any analyses, compilations, or derivatives created by the Recipient that contain or reflect such information. Confidential Information does not include information that: (i) is or becomes publicly available through no breach of this Agreement; (ii) was lawfully in the Recipient’s possession prior to disclosure by the Discloser; (iii) is independently developed by the Recipient without reference to the Discloser’s Confidential Information; or (iv) is rightfully received from a third party without confidentiality restrictions.  

The Recipient acknowledges the sensitive nature of the Confidential Information and agrees to exercise the same degree of care as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but in no event less than reasonable care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: The Recipient may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship with the Discloser, as explicitly agreed in writing.  

2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components or methodologies.  

3. **No Unauthorized Copies**: The Recipient shall not make copies of Confidential Information except as strictly necessary for the authorized purpose, and all copies must bear the same confidentiality markings as the original.  

4. **Restricted Access**: Confidential Information shall only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or agents of the Recipient who have a need-to-know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  

5. **No Public Disclosure**: The Recipient shall not disclose Confidential Information to any third party without the Discloser’s prior written consent, except as required by law.  

6. **Legal Compliance**: If legally compelled to disclose Confidential Information, the Recipient shall promptly notify the Discloser to allow intervention, unless prohibited by law.  

7. **No Competitive Use**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to develop competing products or services or to gain a competitive advantage.  

8. **Security Measures**: The Recipient shall implement and maintain reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

9. **Return or Destruction**: Upon the Discloser’s request or termination of this Agreement, the Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  

10. **No Implied Rights**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Recipient any license, ownership, or rights to the Discloser’s Confidential Information beyond the scope of this Agreement.  

11. **No Misrepresentation**: The Recipient shall not misrepresent the origin or ownership of Confidential Information or claim any rights to it.  

12. **No Subcontracting**: The Recipient shall not subcontract or delegate its obligations under this Agreement without the Discloser’s prior written consent.  

13. **No High-Risk Storage**: Confidential Information shall not be stored on unsecured or publicly accessible systems, including cloud services without encryption.  

14. **Notification of Breach**: The Recipient shall immediately notify the Discloser of any actual or suspected breach of confidentiality and cooperate to mitigate harm.  

15. **Residual Knowledge**: The Recipient may retain generalized knowledge or skills derived from Confidential Information, provided such retention does not violate this Agreement.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., three (3) years] from the effective date (the "Term"). Upon expiration, the Agreement may be renewed by mutual written agreement of both parties, subject to the same or amended terms. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing written notice to the other party, with such termination becoming effective upon receipt of the notice. Notwithstanding termination or expiration, the Recipient’s obligations to protect Confidential Information shall survive for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] from the date of disclosure, or indefinitely for trade secrets as defined under applicable law.  

Early termination of this Agreement does not relieve the Recipient of its obligations regarding Confidential Information disclosed prior to termination. Upon termination or expiration, the Recipient shall promptly cease all use of Confidential Information and, at the Discloser’s election, either return or destroy all materials containing Confidential Information and provide written certification of such destruction. The Discloser reserves the right to audit the Recipient’s compliance with these obligations upon reasonable notice.  

#part 4  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any dispute arising out of or related to this Agreement, including breaches of confidentiality, shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its then-current rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert city, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction.  

Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts located in [insert venue, e.g., the County of San Francisco] for any proceedings ancillary to arbitration or injunctive relief.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 5
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") defines "Confidential Information" as any non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party"), whether in written, oral, electronic, or any other form, that is designated as confidential or that reasonably should be understood to be confidential given the nature of the information or the circumstances of disclosure. Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to:  

1. **Trade Secrets**: Any business, technical, or financial information, including formulas, patterns, compilations, programs, devices, methods, techniques, or processes that derive independent economic value from not being generally known or readily ascertainable.  
2. **Business Strategies**: Plans, forecasts, marketing strategies, customer lists, pricing data, sales pipelines, and other proprietary business information.  
3. **Intellectual Property**: Unpublished patents, copyrights, trademarks, trade dress, and other proprietary rights, including research and development data.  
4. **Technical Data**: Software code, algorithms, schematics, designs, prototypes, technical drawings, and engineering specifications.  
5. **Financial Information**: Revenue, profit margins, budgets, investment strategies, and other financial records not publicly disclosed.  
6. **Personal Data**: Any personally identifiable information (PII) or protected health information (PHI) as defined under applicable privacy laws.  

The scope of this Agreement extends to all Confidential Information shared during the term of this Agreement, including information disclosed prior to the execution of this Agreement if such information is retroactively designated as Confidential Information. Information shall not be considered Confidential Information if it: (a) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Receiving Party; (b) was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession prior to disclosure; (c) is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reference to the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information; or (d) is rightfully obtained from a third party without restriction.  

The Receiving Party acknowledges that unauthorized disclosure or use of Confidential Information could cause irreparable harm to the Disclosing Party, and the Disclosing Party retains all rights to seek equitable relief in addition to any other remedies available under law.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: Confidential Information may only be used for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship between the parties, as explicitly agreed in writing.  
2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components.  
3. **No Unauthorized Copies**: The Receiving Party shall not reproduce Confidential Information except as necessary for the authorized purpose and with proper attribution.  
4. **Restricted Access**: Confidential Information shall only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or agents who have a need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  
5. **No Public Disclosure**: The Receiving Party shall not disclose Confidential Information to the public, media, or third parties without prior written consent.  
6. **Security Measures**: The Receiving Party shall implement reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  
7. **No Competitive Use**: Confidential Information shall not be used to develop competing products, services, or strategies.  
8. **No Modification**: The Receiving Party shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works from Confidential Information without express written permission.  
9. **Notification of Breach**: The Receiving Party shall immediately notify the Disclosing Party upon discovering any unauthorized disclosure or use of Confidential Information.  
10. **Return or Destruction**: Upon request or termination of this Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  
11. **No Implied Licenses**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Receiving Party any rights, title, or interest in Confidential Information beyond the terms herein.  
12. **Compliance with Laws**: The Receiving Party shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations governing the handling of Confidential Information, including data protection laws.  
13. **No Solicitation**: The Receiving Party shall not solicit the Disclosing Party’s employees, customers, or partners using Confidential Information.  
14. **No Sub-Licensing**: The Receiving Party shall not sublicense, assign, or transfer Confidential Information to third parties without prior written consent.  
15. **Audit Rights**: The Disclosing Party may audit the Receiving Party’s compliance with this Agreement upon reasonable notice.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the Effective Date (the "Term"). Upon expiration, the Agreement may be renewed for additional terms by mutual written agreement of the parties. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing thirty (30) days’ written notice to the other party. Notwithstanding termination or expiration, the Receiving Party’s obligations with respect to Confidential Information shall survive for a period of [insert duration, e.g., five (5) years] or as required by applicable law, whichever is longer.  

Termination for breach of this Agreement shall be immediate upon written notice if the breaching party fails to cure such breach within fifteen (15) days of receiving notice. In the event of termination, the Receiving Party shall promptly cease all use of Confidential Information and comply with the return or destruction requirements outlined in Part 2. The Disclosing Party’s remedies for breach shall include injunctive relief, damages, and recovery of attorneys’ fees.  

#part 4  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising under or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association (AAA)] under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert city, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the arbitrator’s decision shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction.  

Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs. The parties waive any right to trial by jury and agree to arbitrate on an individual basis, not as part of a class action or consolidated proceeding.

##prompt_id: 1, type: segmented, sample_id: 6
********
#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure and use of confidential information exchanged between the Disclosing Party and the Receiving Party. For purposes of this Agreement, "Confidential Information" refers to any non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information, whether disclosed orally, in writing, electronically, or in any other form, that is designated as confidential or that, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential. This includes, but is not limited to:  

1. **Business Information**: Trade secrets, business strategies, financial data, pricing models, marketing plans, customer lists, supplier details, and operational methods.  
2. **Technical Information**: Software code, algorithms, patents, inventions, prototypes, research and development data, technical specifications, and engineering designs.  
3. **Legal and Regulatory Information**: Pending or threatened litigation, regulatory filings, compliance reports, and internal audit findings.  
4. **Personal Data**: Any personally identifiable information (PII) or protected health information (PHI) as defined under applicable privacy laws.  

Confidential Information does not include information that: (a) is or becomes publicly available through no breach of this Agreement by the Receiving Party; (b) was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession prior to disclosure by the Disclosing Party; (c) is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reliance on the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information; or (d) is rightfully obtained from a third party without restriction.  

The scope of this Agreement extends to all Confidential Information disclosed during the term of this Agreement, regardless of the medium or method of disclosure. The Receiving Party agrees to treat such information with at least the same degree of care as it accords to its own confidential information, but no less than a reasonable standard of care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Use**: Confidential Information may only be used for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship between the Parties, as explicitly agreed in writing.  
2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information provided in tangible or electronic form.  
3. **No Unauthorized Copies**: The Receiving Party shall not make copies of Confidential Information except as necessary for authorized use, and such copies shall bear the same confidentiality markings as the original.  
4. **Limited Disclosure**: Confidential Information may only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or advisors who have a need-to-know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as stringent as this Agreement.  
5. **No Publicity**: Neither Party shall issue press releases or public announcements regarding the existence or terms of this Agreement without prior written consent.  
6. **Data Security**: The Receiving Party shall implement reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  
7. **No Transfer of Rights**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Receiving Party any ownership or license rights in the Confidential Information, except as expressly stated.  
8. **Compliance with Laws**: The Receiving Party shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations, including export control and data protection laws, when handling Confidential Information.  
9. **Notification of Breach**: The Receiving Party shall immediately notify the Disclosing Party upon discovering any unauthorized use or disclosure of Confidential Information.  
10. **Return or Destruction**: Upon request or termination of this Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify such destruction in writing.  
11. **No Solicitation**: During the term of this Agreement and for one year thereafter, the Receiving Party shall not solicit the Disclosing Party’s employees or contractors.  
12. **No Competitive Use**: Confidential Information shall not be used to develop, market, or sell competing products or services.  
13. **Third-Party Confidentiality**: The Receiving Party shall ensure that any third parties to whom Confidential Information is disclosed adhere to the terms of this Agreement.  
14. **No Modification**: The Receiving Party shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works based on Confidential Information without prior written consent.  
15. **Survival of Obligations**: The obligations under this section shall survive termination of this Agreement for the duration specified in Part 3.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall commence on the Effective Date and remain in full force and effect for a period of [●] years ("Initial Term"), unless terminated earlier as provided herein. Upon expiration of the Initial Term, this Agreement may be renewed for successive [●]-year terms ("Renewal Terms") by mutual written agreement of the Parties. Either Party may terminate this Agreement at any time, with or without cause, by providing [●] days’ prior written notice to the other Party. Termination of this Agreement shall not relieve the Receiving Party of its obligations with respect to Confidential Information disclosed during the term of the Agreement.  

Notwithstanding termination, the Receiving Party’s duty to protect Confidential Information shall survive for a period of [●] years from the date of termination, except for trade secrets, which shall be protected indefinitely until such information ceases to qualify as a trade secret under applicable law. Upon termination, the Receiving Party shall, at the Disclosing Party’s option, promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and provide written certification of such destruction. The Parties agree that monetary damages may not be a sufficient remedy for breach of this Agreement, and the Disclosing Party shall be entitled to seek injunctive or equitable relief without posting a bond.  

#part 4  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [●], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or relating to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [●] under its then-current rules, and judgment on the award rendered by the arbitrator(s) may be entered in any court having jurisdiction thereof. The arbitration shall be conducted in [●], and the language of the arbitration shall be [●]. Each Party shall bear its own costs and expenses, including attorney fees, unless the arbitrator(s) determine that a Party has acted in bad faith, in which case the prevailing Party shall be entitled to recover its reasonable costs and fees. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either Party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm. The Parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts located in [●] for such purposes.

#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") defines "Confidential Information" as any non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party"), whether in written, oral, electronic, or other form, and regardless of whether such information is marked or identified as confidential. Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to: (a) trade secrets, business strategies, financial data, marketing plans, and operational processes; (b) technical information, such as software code, algorithms, patents, and product designs; (c) customer or client lists, pricing models, and contractual terms; (d) any other information that, by its nature or the circumstances of its disclosure, should reasonably be understood as confidential.  

The scope of this Agreement extends to all Confidential Information shared between the parties during the term of this Agreement, including information disclosed prior to the execution of this Agreement if such information was shared under circumstances implying confidentiality. Confidential Information does not include information that: (a) is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Receiving Party; (b) was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession prior to disclosure by the Disclosing Party; (c) is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reference to the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information; or (d) is rightfully obtained by the Receiving Party from a third party without restriction.  

The Receiving Party acknowledges that unauthorized disclosure or use of Confidential Information could cause irreparable harm to the Disclosing Party. Accordingly, the Receiving Party agrees to exercise the same degree of care to protect Confidential Information as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than a reasonable standard of care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Use**: The Receiving Party may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship with the Disclosing Party, as explicitly agreed in writing.  
2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Receiving Party shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components.  
3. **No Unauthorized Copies**: The Receiving Party shall not make copies of Confidential Information except as necessary for authorized use, and all copies must bear the same confidentiality markings as the original.  
4. **Limited Disclosure**: Confidential Information may only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or advisors who have a need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  
5. **No Publicity**: The Receiving Party shall not issue press releases or public statements referencing the Disclosing Party or the Confidential Information without prior written consent.  
6. **Data Security**: The Receiving Party shall implement appropriate technical and organizational measures to safeguard Confidential Information against unauthorized access or breaches.  
7. **No Transfer of Rights**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Receiving Party any intellectual property rights or licenses to the Confidential Information.  
8. **No Competitive Use**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to develop competing products or services.  
9. **Compliance with Laws**: The Receiving Party shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection laws.  
10. **Notification of Breach**: The Receiving Party must promptly notify the Disclosing Party upon discovering any unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information.  
11. **Return or Destruction**: Upon request or termination of this Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  
12. **No Third-Party Sharing**: Confidential Information shall not be shared with third parties unless expressly permitted by the Disclosing Party in writing.  
13. **No Misrepresentation**: The Receiving Party shall not misrepresent the origin or ownership of Confidential Information.  
14. **No Circumvention**: The Receiving Party shall not use Confidential Information to circumvent the Disclosing Party’s business relationships or opportunities.  
15. **Audit Rights**: The Disclosing Party may audit the Receiving Party’s compliance with this Agreement upon reasonable notice.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the Effective Date (the "Term"). The Term may be renewed by mutual written agreement of both parties for additional periods of equal or shorter duration. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing written notice to the other party, with such termination becoming effective upon receipt of the notice. Notwithstanding termination, the obligations of confidentiality shall survive for a period of [insert duration, e.g., three (3) years] after the termination date, except for trade secrets, which shall remain protected indefinitely under applicable law. Upon termination, the Receiving Party shall cease all use of Confidential Information and, as directed by the Disclosing Party, return or destroy all materials containing Confidential Information. The Disclosing Party may require the Receiving Party to provide written certification of such destruction. Any provisions of this Agreement that, by their nature, should survive termination (e.g., confidentiality obligations, dispute resolution, and governing law) shall remain in effect.  

#part 4

#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information (collectively, "Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, any data, materials, documents, trade secrets, business strategies, financial information, technical specifications, product designs, software, algorithms, customer lists, marketing plans, or any other information disclosed in written, oral, electronic, or any other form, whether or not marked as confidential.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all information shared by the Discloser, whether directly or indirectly, in the course of discussions, negotiations, or collaborations between the parties. This includes information shared during meetings, presentations, emails, or any other communication, as well as information derived or generated from such disclosures. Confidential Information also encompasses any analyses, compilations, summaries, or other materials prepared by the Recipient that contain or reflect the Discloser’s Confidential Information.  

Exclusions from Confidential Information include: (1) information already known to the Recipient at the time of disclosure, as evidenced by written records; (2) information publicly available or becoming publicly available without breach of this Agreement; (3) information lawfully obtained from a third party without confidentiality obligations; or (4) information independently developed by the Recipient without reference to the Discloser’s Confidential Information.  

The Recipient acknowledges the sensitive nature of the Confidential Information and agrees to exercise the same degree of care as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than reasonable care. The Recipient shall not disclose, reproduce, or use the Confidential Information for any purpose other than as expressly permitted under this Agreement.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Purpose**: The Recipient may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a potential business relationship with the Discloser, as mutually agreed in writing.  

2. **No Reverse Engineering**: The Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to discover underlying trade secrets or proprietary methods.  

3. **Limited Access**: Confidential Information shall only be disclosed to employees, contractors, or agents of the Recipient who have a legitimate need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  

4. **No Unauthorized Copies**: The Recipient shall not make copies of Confidential Information except as strictly necessary for the authorized purpose, and all copies must bear the same confidentiality markings as the original.  

5. **No Public Disclosure**: The Recipient shall not publish, distribute, or otherwise make Confidential Information available to the public or any third party without the Discloser’s prior written consent.  

6. **No Competitive Use**: The Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to develop, market, or sell competing products or services.  

7. **Security Measures**: The Recipient shall implement appropriate physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

8. **Notification of Breach**: The Recipient shall immediately notify the Discloser upon discovering any unauthorized disclosure or misuse of Confidential Information and take all reasonable steps to mitigate harm.  

9. **No License Grant**: Nothing in this Agreement grants the Recipient any license, ownership, or rights to the Discloser’s Confidential Information beyond the limited use permitted herein.  

10. **Compliance with Laws**: The Recipient shall comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection and export control laws.  

11. **No Solicitation**: The Recipient shall not solicit or hire the Discloser’s employees, contractors, or customers using Confidential Information.  

12. **Return or Destruction**: Upon the Discloser’s request or termination of this Agreement, the Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  

13. **No Misrepresentation**: The Recipient shall not misrepresent the origin, ownership, or accuracy of Confidential Information.  

14. **No Assignment**: The Recipient shall not assign or transfer its rights or obligations under this Agreement without the Discloser’s prior written consent.  

15. **Survival of Obligations**: The Recipient’s confidentiality obligations shall survive termination of this Agreement for the duration specified in Part 3.  

#part 3  
**Term, Renewal, and Termination**  

This Agreement shall remain in effect for a period of [insert duration, e.g., two (2) years] from the Effective Date ("Term"). Upon expiration of the Term, the Agreement may be renewed by mutual written agreement of the parties, subject to the same terms and conditions or as otherwise agreed. Either party may terminate this Agreement at any time by providing written notice to the other party, with such termination effective upon receipt of the notice.  

Notwithstanding termination or expiration, the Recipient’s obligations to protect Confidential Information shall survive for a period of [insert duration, e.g., three (3) years] from the date of disclosure, unless otherwise required by law or agreed in writing. Upon termination, the Recipient shall cease all use of Confidential Information and, at the Discloser’s option, return or destroy all copies of Confidential Information in its possession or control. The Recipient shall provide written certification of such destruction upon request.  

The Discloser may terminate this Agreement immediately upon written notice if the Recipient breaches any of its obligations hereunder. Termination shall not relieve the Recipient of its obligations with respect to Confidential Information disclosed prior to termination. Any provisions of this Agreement that, by their nature, should survive termination (e.g., confidentiality obligations, dispute resolution, and governing law) shall remain in effect.  

#part 4  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [insert jurisdiction, e.g., the State of California], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [insert arbitration institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association] under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [insert city, e.g., San Francisco, California], and the award rendered by the arbitrator(s) shall be final and binding upon the parties. Judgment on the award may be entered in any court of competent jurisdiction.  

Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations pending arbitration. The parties waive any right to a jury trial in any action or proceeding related to this Agreement. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in connection with such dispute. This clause shall survive termination or expiration of this Agreement.

Confidential Information excludes: (i) information already known to the Recipient at the time of disclosure; (ii) information lawfully obtained from a third party without breach of confidentiality; (iii) information independently developed by the Recipient without reference to the Discloser’s Confidential Information; or (iv) information that becomes publicly available through no fault of the Recipient.

#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement ("Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information ("Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information refers to any data, material, or knowledge, whether tangible or intangible, disclosed in any form (written, oral, electronic, or otherwise) that is marked or designated as confidential or that, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to:  
- Trade secrets, business strategies, marketing plans, financial data, and forecasts.  
- Technical information, such as software code, algorithms, patents, inventions, and research.  
- Product designs, prototypes, specifications, and manufacturing processes.  
- Customer lists, supplier details, pricing models, and contractual terms.  
- Any other proprietary information not publicly available or generally known in the industry.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all derivatives, analyses, or compilations created by the Recipient that incorporate or reflect such information. However, Confidential Information does not include information that:  
- Was lawfully in the Recipient’s possession prior to disclosure.  
- Becomes publicly available through no fault of the Recipient.  
- Is independently developed by the Recipient without reliance on the Discloser’s Confidential Information.  
- Is rightfully received from a third party without restriction on disclosure.  

The Recipient acknowledges the sensitive nature of the Confidential Information and agrees to exercise the same degree of care as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than reasonable care. The obligations under this Agreement survive for a period of [X] years from the date of disclosure, unless otherwise required by law.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Use**: Confidential Information may only be used for the purpose of evaluating or pursuing a business relationship between the parties, as explicitly agreed in writing.  
2. **No Reverse Engineering**: Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components.  
3. **No Unauthorized Copies**: Recipient may not make copies of Confidential Information except as necessary for authorized use, and all copies must include proprietary notices.  
4. **Limited Disclosure**: Confidential Information may only be disclosed to employees, agents, or contractors with a need-to-know, provided they are bound by similar confidentiality obligations.  
5. **No Publicity**: Recipient shall not issue press releases or public statements referencing the Discloser or the Confidential Information without prior written consent.  
6. **Data Security**: Recipient must implement industry-standard security measures to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or breaches.  
7. **No Competitive Use**: Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to develop competing products or services.  
8. **No Transfer of Rights**: This Agreement does not grant Recipient any intellectual property rights, licenses, or ownership in the Confidential Information.  
9. **Return or Destroy**: Upon request, Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all Confidential Information and certify its destruction in writing.  
10. **No Circumvention**: Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to bypass or undermine the Discloser’s business relationships or opportunities.  
11. **Compliance with Laws**: Recipient must comply with all applicable laws and regulations in handling Confidential Information, including data protection laws.  
12. **No Misrepresentation**: Recipient shall not misrepresent the origin or accuracy of Confidential Information.  
13. **Notification of Breach**: Recipient must immediately notify Discloser of any unauthorized disclosure or breach and cooperate to mitigate harm.  
14. **No Sub-Licensing**: Recipient may not sublicense, assign, or transfer Confidential Information to third parties without Discloser’s prior written consent.  
15. **Audit Rights**: Discloser may audit Recipient’s compliance with this Agreement upon reasonable notice.  

#part 3  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [State/Country], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or related to this Agreement shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [Arbitration Institution, e.g., AAA] under its commercial rules. The arbitration shall be conducted in [City, State/Country], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. The prevailing party in any arbitration or legal proceeding shall be entitled to recover reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in a court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations. The parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the state and federal courts located in [County, State/Country] for such purposes. This clause survives termination of the Agreement.

#part 1  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement (the "Agreement") governs the disclosure of confidential and proprietary information (collectively, "Confidential Information") between the disclosing party ("Discloser") and the receiving party ("Recipient"). Confidential Information includes, but is not limited to, all non-public, sensitive, or proprietary information, whether disclosed orally, in writing, electronically, or by any other means, that is designated as confidential or that, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

Confidential Information encompasses, without limitation: (a) trade secrets, business strategies, marketing plans, financial data, and forecasts; (b) technical information, including software, algorithms, patents, inventions, and research and development; (c) customer and supplier lists, pricing structures, and contractual terms; (d) any other information that derives independent economic value from not being generally known or readily ascertainable by others; and (e) any analyses, compilations, or summaries derived from such information.  

The scope of Confidential Information extends to all forms of communication, including written documents, electronic files, verbal discussions, and demonstrations. However, Confidential Information does not include information that: (i) is or becomes publicly available through no breach of this Agreement by Recipient; (ii) was lawfully in Recipient’s possession prior to disclosure by Discloser; (iii) is independently developed by Recipient without reliance on Discloser’s Confidential Information; or (iv) is rightfully obtained by Recipient from a third party without restriction.  

Recipient acknowledges that Confidential Information is valuable and that unauthorized disclosure or use could cause irreparable harm to Discloser. Accordingly, Recipient agrees to exercise the same degree of care to protect Confidential Information as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than a reasonable standard of care.  

#part 2  
**Permitted Uses and Restrictions**  

1. **Authorized Use**: Recipient may use Confidential Information solely for the purpose of evaluating or engaging in a business relationship with Discloser, as explicitly agreed upon in writing.  

2. **No Reverse Engineering**: Recipient shall not reverse engineer, decompile, or disassemble any Confidential Information to derive its underlying components or methodologies.  

3. **No Unauthorized Copying**: Recipient shall not copy, reproduce, or duplicate Confidential Information except as strictly necessary for the permitted use and only with Discloser’s prior written consent.  

4. **Limited Disclosure**: Recipient may disclose Confidential Information only to its employees, agents, or advisors who have a need to know and are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as this Agreement.  

5. **No Publicity**: Recipient shall not issue press releases, marketing materials, or other public statements referencing Discloser or the Confidential Information without Discloser’s express written approval.  

6. **Data Security**: Recipient shall implement and maintain reasonable physical, technical, and administrative safeguards to protect Confidential Information from unauthorized access or disclosure.  

7. **No Transfer of Rights**: Nothing in this Agreement grants Recipient any rights, title, or interest in or to Confidential Information, which remains the exclusive property of Discloser.  

8. **Return or Destruction**: Upon Discloser’s request or termination of this Agreement, Recipient shall promptly return or destroy all copies of Confidential Information and certify such destruction in writing.  

9. **No Competitive Use**: Recipient shall not use Confidential Information to develop, market, or sell products or services that compete with Discloser’s business.  

10. **Compliance with Laws**: Recipient shall comply with all applicable laws, regulations, and industry standards in handling Confidential Information, including data protection laws.  

11. **No Subcontracting**: Recipient shall not disclose Confidential Information to subcontractors or third-party vendors without Discloser’s prior written consent.  

12. **Notification of Breach**: Recipient shall immediately notify Discloser in writing upon discovering any unauthorized access, use, or disclosure of Confidential Information.  

13. **No Modification**: Recipient shall not alter, modify, or create derivative works based on Confidential Information without Discloser’s express written permission.  

14. **Duration of Obligations**: Recipient’s confidentiality obligations shall survive termination of this Agreement for a period of [X] years, unless otherwise required by law.  

15. **No Implied Licenses**: No license or right is granted under any patents, copyrights, or other intellectual property rights embodied in Confidential Information, except as expressly stated herein.  

#part 3  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of [Specify State], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or related to this Agreement, including its interpretation, enforcement, or breach, shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by the American Arbitration Association (AAA) under its Commercial Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall take place in [Specify City, State], and the arbitrator’s decision shall be final and binding. Judgment on the arbitration award may be entered in any court of competent jurisdiction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or enforce confidentiality obligations. The prevailing party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in connection with such dispute. The parties irrevocably waive any right to a jury trial and agree that arbitration shall be the sole and exclusive forum for resolving disputes under this Agreement.

##prompt_id: 3, type: segmented, sample_id: 1
********
#part 1  
**NON-DISCLOSURE AGREEMENT**  
**Definition and Scope of Confidential Information**  

1. **Definition of Confidential Information**  
For the purposes of this Agreement, "Confidential Information" shall mean any and all non-public, proprietary, or sensitive information, whether in written, oral, electronic, or other form, disclosed by one party (the "Disclosing Party") to the other party (the "Receiving Party"), including but not limited to:  
   (a) Business plans, strategies, financial data, forecasts, and market analyses;  
   (b) Technical data, trade secrets, inventions, patents, copyrights, and know-how;  
   (c) Customer lists, supplier information, pricing structures, and contractual terms;  
   (d) Software, algorithms, source code, and other intellectual property;  
   (e) Any other information marked or designated as confidential or which, by its nature, should reasonably be understood to be confidential.  

2. **Exclusions**  
Confidential Information shall not include information that:  
   (a) Is or becomes publicly available through no fault of the Receiving Party;  
   (b) Was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession prior to disclosure by the Disclosing Party;  
   (c) Is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reliance on the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information; or  
   (d) Is rightfully obtained by the Receiving Party from a third party without breach of any confidentiality obligation.  

3. **Obligations of the Receiving Party**  
The Receiving Party agrees to:  
   (a) Maintain the confidentiality of the Disclosing Party’s Confidential Information with at least the same degree of care as it uses to protect its own confidential information, but no less than a reasonable standard of care;  
   (b) Use the Confidential Information solely for the purpose for which it was disclosed and not for any other purpose without the Disclosing Party’s prior written consent;  
   (c) Restrict access to the Confidential Information to its employees, agents, or representatives who have a need to know and who are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as restrictive as those herein;  
   (d) Not disclose, reproduce, or distribute the Confidential Information to any third party without the Disclosing Party’s express written permission.  

4. **Duration of Confidentiality Obligations**  
The Receiving Party’s obligations under this Agreement shall survive for a period of [X] years from the date of disclosure, except for trade secrets, which shall remain protected indefinitely until they no longer qualify as trade secrets under applicable law.  

5. **Return or Destruction of Confidential Information**  
Upon the Disclosing Party’s written request or upon termination of this Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all copies of the Confidential Information and certify in writing such destruction, except as required by law or internal compliance policies.  

#part 2  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [State/Country], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any dispute, controversy, or claim arising out of or relating to this Agreement, including its breach, termination, or validity, shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [Arbitration Institution, e.g., the American Arbitration Association (AAA)] in accordance with its [applicable rules, e.g., Commercial Arbitration Rules]. The arbitration shall be conducted in [City, State/Country], and the arbitral award shall be final and binding upon both parties. Judgment upon the award rendered by the arbitrator(s) may be entered in any court having jurisdiction thereof. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either party may seek injunctive relief in any court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm or preserve rights pending arbitration. The prevailing party in any arbitration or legal proceeding shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in connection with such proceeding. The parties hereby waive any right to a jury trial and agree to arbitrate solely on an individual basis, with no class or representative actions permitted.

   - Not disclose, reproduce, or distribute the Confidential Information to any third party without the Disclosing Party’s prior written consent.  

4. **Duration of Confidentiality Obligations**  
The Receiving Party’s obligations under this Agreement shall survive for a period of [X] years from the date of disclosure, except for trade secrets, which shall remain protected for as long as they qualify as trade secrets under applicable law.  

5. **Return or Destruction of Confidential Information**  
Upon the Disclosing Party’s written request or upon termination of this Agreement, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all copies of Confidential Information and certify in writing such destruction, except as required by law or internal compliance policies.  

#part 2  
**Jurisdiction, Governing Law, and Dispute Resolution**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [State/Country], without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any disputes arising out of or relating to this Agreement, including its interpretation or breach, shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [Arbitration Institution, e.g., AAA or JAMS] under its then-current rules. The arbitration shall be conducted in [City, State/Country], and the arbitral award shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. Alternatively, if arbitration is not enforceable, the parties irrevocably submit to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts located in [County, State/Country] for the resolution of any disputes. The prevailing party in any arbitration or litigation shall be entitled to recover its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs incurred in connection with such proceeding. This clause survives termination of the Agreement.

##prompt_id: 3, type: segmented, sample_id: 4
********
#part 1  
**NON-DISCLOSURE AGREEMENT**  
**DEFINITION AND SCOPE OF CONFIDENTIAL INFORMATION**  

This Non-Disclosure Agreement ("Agreement") is entered into by and between the Disclosing Party and the Receiving Party (collectively, the "Parties") to protect certain confidential and proprietary information disclosed during their business relationship.  

**1. Definition of Confidential Information**  
Confidential Information ("CI") refers to any data, material, or knowledge, whether tangible or intangible, disclosed by the Disclosing Party to the Receiving Party, which is not generally known to the public and is marked or identified as confidential or proprietary at the time of disclosure. CI includes, but is not limited to:  
- Trade secrets, business strategies, and financial information.  
- Technical data, prototypes, software, algorithms, and research.  
- Customer lists, marketing plans, and contractual terms.  
- Any other information that, by its nature or circumstances of disclosure, should reasonably be understood as confidential.  

**2. Exclusions**  
CI shall not include information that:  
- Was lawfully in the Receiving Party’s possession prior to disclosure.  
- Becomes publicly available without breach of this Agreement.  
- Is independently developed by the Receiving Party without reliance on the Disclosing Party’s CI.  
- Is rightfully obtained from a third party without confidentiality obligations.  

**3. Obligations of the Receiving Party**  
The Receiving Party agrees to:  
- Maintain the confidentiality of CI using at least the same degree of care as it uses for its own confidential information, but no less than reasonable care.  
- Restrict access to CI to employees, agents, or representatives with a need-to-know basis, who are bound by confidentiality obligations at least as stringent as those herein.  
- Refrain from copying, reverse-engineering, or exploiting CI for any purpose other than the agreed-upon business relationship.  

**4. Term and Return of Materials**  
This Agreement shall remain in effect for [●] years from the date of disclosure, unless otherwise terminated in writing. Upon termination or request, the Receiving Party shall promptly return or destroy all CI and certify its destruction in writing.  

**5. Remedies**  
The Parties acknowledge that unauthorized disclosure of CI may cause irreparable harm, entitling the Disclosing Party to seek injunctive relief in addition to monetary damages.  

#part 2  
**JURISDICTION, GOVERNING LAW, AND DISPUTE RESOLUTION**  

This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of [●] without regard to its conflict of laws principles. Any dispute arising out of or relating to this Agreement, including its breach, termination, or validity, shall be resolved exclusively through binding arbitration administered by [● Arbitration Institution] under its then-current rules. The arbitration shall be conducted in [● City, State/Country], and the award rendered shall be final and enforceable in any court of competent jurisdiction. The Parties waive any right to a jury trial or to litigate in court, except to enforce an arbitration award or seek injunctive relief. Notwithstanding the foregoing, either Party may seek provisional remedies in a court of competent jurisdiction to prevent irreparable harm pending arbitration. The prevailing Party in any dispute shall be entitled to recover reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs. This clause survives termination of the Agreement.
